|---|---|---|---|---|---|
|Quantity|Symboll<br>Equation|MKS unit|Quantity|Symboll<br>Equation|MKS unit|
|Length|_s_|meter (m)|Angular<br>displacement|6|radian (rad)|
|Mass|_M_|kilogram (kg)|Moment of<br>inertia|_J=Jr 2dm_|kg'm2|
|Velocity|_vvdsjdt_|_meterl_second<br>_(m/s)_|Angular<br>velocity|_w=d6/dt_|rad/s|
|Acceleration|_avdv[dt_|_m/s2_|Angular<br>acceleration|_a=dw/dt_|rad/s2|
|Force|_F=Ma_|newton (N)|Torque|_T=Ja_|newton-meter<br>(Nrn) or J/rad|
|Work|_W=JFds_|joule (1)|Work|_W=JTd6_|J, or W's|
|Power|_p=dW/dt_<br>_=Fv_|watt (W)|Power|_p=dW/dt_<br>_=Tw_|W|

||_X"_<br>_q_|0.2 - 0.45|0.12 - 0.25|

||_Tq'o_|-|0.5 - 2.0 s|
